<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Dear Mr. Owings:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We submit this letter in response to the comments
from the staff of the Division of Corporation Finance of the SEC, received by
letter dated June 21, 2010, pertaining to the referenced Form 10-K and
definitive proxy statement.&#160; The staff&#146;s
comments are reproduced below, followed by our responses.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Form 10-K for the Fiscal Year Ended January 30, 2010</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 7.&#160;
Management&#146;s Discussion and Analysis of Financial Condition, page 11</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Results of Operations, page 12</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We note that you do not provide a discussion and analysis of changes in
sales for each year presented.&#160; We also
note that you do not quantify the impact of a number of factors that
contributed to the change in total sales for the most recent year.&#160; Please provide a discussion and analysis of
sales for each year presented.&#160; Also,
please clarify your disclosure regarding the </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\mweinst\10-14138-1\task4187754\14138-1-bi-01.htm',USER='mweinst',CD='Jul 15 12:39 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">reasons for the change in total sales for the most
recent year since it appears that a decline in retail fuel prices would not
have the effect of increasing total sales.&#160;
In addition, it would be useful to investors to understand (a) the
effect of changes in transaction counts and average sale per shopping trip in
your analysis of identical supermarket sales, excluding fuel, (b) the reasons
for the changes in the retail price of fuel, and (c) the effect of the change
in retail square footage.&#160; Further, since
you include both identical and comparable supermarket sales in your discussion,
please discuss both of these operating metrics in your analysis.&#160; Finally, please provide a discussion and
analysis of other sales to the extent changes in such sales is significant to
the overall change between years.&#160;
Alternatively, please tell us why you believe enhanced disclosure is not
useful to investors.&#160; Please refer to
Item 303(a)(3) of Regulation S-K and Section III.B.4 of SEC Release No.
34-48960.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger Response</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We propose to add disclosure in future filings for
all periods and years presented, so that in next year&#146;s Form 10-K, comparisons
will be made between 2010 and 2009, and between 2009 and 2008, comparable to
the following:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;The slight increase in total sales for 2009
compared to 2008 was attributable to our 2.1% increase in identical sales
offset by our year-over-year decline in supermarket fuel sales of approximately
10.6%.&#160; Total supermarket fuel sales
declined over the same period due to a decline in retail fuel prices of
approximately 40%, offset partially by a 17.2% increase in gallons sold.&#160; Retail fuel prices decreased by approximately
40% year-over-year in 2009 compared to 2008 due to deflation in the product
cost of fuel.&#160; The increase in total supermarket
sales without fuel for 2009 over 2008 was primarily the result of increases in
identical supermarket sales of 2.1% as well as an increase in supermarket
square footage of 0.8%.&#160; Identical
supermarket sales, excluding fuel, increased due to increased transaction count
offset partially by a lower average sale per shopping trip.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Comparable store sales represent approximately 99%
of total supermarket sales for 2009, 2008, and 2007, so we do not believe that
it is useful for us to differentiate between total supermarket sales and
comparable store sales.&#160; The change in
other sales is not material to Kroger&#146;s financial statements, therefore,
additional discussion is not meaningful to investors and is unwarranted.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Liquidity and Capital Resources, page 21</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We note the disclosure on page 26 that you believe cash flow from
operations and other sources of liquidity, including borrowings under your
commercial paper program and bank credit facility will be adequate to meet
anticipated requirements for working capital, capital expenditures, interest
payments and scheduled principal payments for the foreseeable future.&#160; Please provide a discussion of prospective
information regarding your short-term and long-term sources and needs for
capital in this section.&#160; Please refer to
Instructions 2 and 5 to Item 303(a) of Regulation S-K and Section 503.a of
Codification of Financial Reporting policies.&#160;
In addition, please provide a discussion of short-term liquidity and
capital resources that cover cash needs for up to 12 months in the future.&#160; A discussion of long-term liquidity and
capital resources should address material capital expenditures, payments due on
long-term debt and other demands or commitments beyond the next 12 months.&#160; Alternatively, tell us why you believe
enhanced disclosure is not useful to investors in understanding your liquidity
and capital resources.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\mweinst\10-14138-1\task4187754\14138-1-bi-01.htm',USER='mweinst',CD='Jul 15 12:39 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger Response</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our current sources of liquidity are cash flows from
operating activities, borrowings under our commercial paper program, and our
bank credit facility. Kroger generated $2.9 billion in cash flows from operating
activities in 2009, has no borrowings under its $2.5 billion revolving credit
facility, has access to commercial paper markets, and currently is authorized
by its board of directors to issue $600 million of securities.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In future filings, Kroger will enhance its
disclosure as follows:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We estimate our liquidity needs over the next
twelve month period to be approximately $3 billion, which includes anticipated
requirements for working capital, capital expenditures, interest payments, and
scheduled principal payments of debt.&#160;
Based on current operating trends, we believe that cash flows from
operating activities and other sources of liquidity, including borrowings under
our commercial paper program and bank credit facility, will be adequate to meet
our liquidity needs for the next twelve months and for the foreseeable future
beyond the next twelve months. In addition to the sources of liquidity noted
above, we also expect to be able to fund future scheduled principal payments of
long-term debt (see Note 5) from our cash flows from operating activities and,
if necessary, by issuing additional senior notes.&#160; We believe we have adequate coverage of our
debt covenants to continue to maintain our current debt ratings and to respond
effectively to competitive conditions.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Outlook, page 26</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We note your disclosure regarding expected bad debt expense from the
credit extended to your customers through your branded credit card.&#160; Please tell us more about this program and
what consideration you gave to disclosing information about the credit card
portfolio and your accounting policies in your discussion and analysis and/or
the notes to consolidated financial statements.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger Response</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For fiscal years ended January 30, 2010 and prior,
our branded credit card was issued by a financial institution not affiliated
with The Kroger Co., on the behalf of the Kroger Personal Finance joint venture
(&#147;KPF&#148;).&#160; As of January 30, 2010, Kroger
and the financial institution each had a 50% interest in KPF.&#160; The financial institution owns the credit
card portfolio and controls the underlying credit policies.&#160; KPF is responsible for marketing the branded
credit card.&#160; The financial institution
is responsible for recording and reporting expenses and revenues associated
with the branded credit card.&#160; Kroger
shares all revenues and expenses related to the credit card portfolio with the
financial institution by virtue of its ownership interest in KPF.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">KPF is a variable interest entity of which we are
not the primary beneficiary.&#160; As such, we
do not consolidate the entity and we account for the entity under the equity
method of accounting.&#160; This entity is
immaterial to our financial statements and, therefore, we do not disclose
additional information regarding the credit card portfolio.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The disclosure related to our share of expected bad
debt expense from the credit card portfolio was disclosed in the Outlook
section.&#160; Due to the credit crisis in
2007, several investors inquired about the Kroger exposure to bad debt
write-offs related to the branded credit card.&#160;
As a result, we disclosed our share of the expected bad debt expense
related to the branded credit card beginning with our Form 10-K for the year
ended February 2, 2008.&#160; Since the
economy has not fully recovered, we have continued to disclose this amount in
Outlook.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 8.&#160;
Financial Statements and Supplementary Data, page 32</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Consolidated Statements of Cash Flows, page 35</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We note that deferred income taxes included in adjustments to reconcile

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Notes to Consolidated Financial Statements, page 37</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">13.&#160; Benefit
Plans, page 57</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Please disclose how you calculate the market related value of plan assets
as that term is defined in ASC 715-30-20.&#160;
Since there is an alternative to how you can calculate this item, and it
has a direct effect on pension expense, we believe you should disclose how you
determine this amount in accordance with FASB ASC 235-10-50-3.</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger Response</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In future filings we will revise our disclosure,
consistent with that shown below, to clarify how we calculate the market
related value of plan assets:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;The Company calculates its expected return on plan
assets by using market related value of plan assets.&#160; The market related value of plan assets is
determined by adjusting the actual fair value of plan assets for unrecognized
gains or losses on plan assets.&#160;
Unrecognized gains or losses represent the difference between actual and
expected returns on plan investments for each plan year.&#160; Unrecognized gains or losses on plan assets
are recognized evenly over a five year period.&#160;
Using a different method to calculate the market related value of plan
assets would provide a different expected return on plan assets.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note 18, Quarterly Data, page 72</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Please disclose gross profit or cost of revenues for each quarter.&#160; Refer to Item 302(a)(1) of Regulation S-K and
Question 3 of SAB Topic 6.G.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger Response</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In future filings, we will begin disclosing our
quarterly unaudited data in the same format as our audited Consolidated
Statements of Operations, as shown below.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The two tables that follow reflect the unaudited
results of operations for 2009 and 2008.</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 15.&#160;
Exhibits, Financial Statement Schedules, page&nbsp;78</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">It appears that you have not provided all of the schedules and/or
exhibits to Exhibit&nbsp;10.11 &#151; Five Year Credit Agreement dated as of November&nbsp;15,
2006, such as Exhibit&nbsp;D &#151; Administrative Questionnaire and Exhibit&nbsp;E &#151;
Guarantee Agreement.&#160; Please re-file the
complete credit agreement, including all schedules and exhibits with your next
periodic report.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger Response</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On June&nbsp;28, 2010, we re-filed the Five Year
Credit Agreement, including all schedules and exhibits, as Exhibit&nbsp;10.11
to our Form&nbsp;10-Q for the Quarterly Period Ended May&nbsp;22, 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Definitive Proxy Statement on Schedule 14A</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Information Concerning the Board of Directors, page&nbsp;15</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Committees of the Board, page&nbsp;15</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We note that you consider racial, ethnic, and gender diversity when
evaluating candidates to serve on your board of directors.&#160; Please describe how you implement this policy
and how you assess the effectiveness of your policy.&#160; Please refer to Item 407(c)(2)(vi)&nbsp;of
Regulation S-K.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\105627\10-14138-1\task4187636\14138-1-bi-03.htm',USER='105627',CD='Jul 15 21:39 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger Response</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As disclosed, the Corporate Governance Committee
considers, among other things, racial, ethnic, and gender diversity when
evaluating candidates to serve on the board of directors.&#160; The Committee has no specific policy
governing how diversity will be considered, and it reviews all potential
nominees based on the totality of their individual qualifications and skills,
taking into account not only diversity but also other skills and attributes
that are to be considered under <i>The Kroger Co. Board of
Directors Guidelines on Issues of Corporate Governance</i>, which can be
viewed on Kroger&#146;s website (www.thekrogerco.com).&#160; As part of an annual review each committee
and the board of directors as a whole evaluate their effectiveness in
fulfilling their responsibilities.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Compensation Policies as they Relate to Risk
Management, page&nbsp;43</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We note your disclosure in response to Item 402(s)&nbsp;of Regulation
S-K.&#160; Please describe the policy you
undertook to reach the conclusion that disclosure was not necessary.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger Response</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As disclosed on page&nbsp;18 of Kroger&#146;s definitive
proxy statement, the Audit Committee has oversight responsibility for the
effectiveness of management&#146;s processes that monitor and manage key business
risks facing Kroger, as well as the major areas of risk exposure and management&#146;s
efforts to monitor and control that exposure.&#160;
In connection with that oversight responsibility, the Audit Committee
discusses with management its policies with respect to risk assessment and risk
management.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Management provides regular updates to the
Compensation Committee throughout the year regarding the management of risks
related to compensation policies.&#160; The
Compensation Committee, in turn, reports on these risks to the full board of
directors.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger&#146;s compensation policies have been designed to
attract and retain highly qualified and engaged employees, and to minimize
risks that would have a material adverse effect on Kroger.&#160; Our compensation programs are designed to
incentivize employees without encouraging excessive risk taking, and those
programs contain the following features that are intended to mitigate risk:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.35pt;text-indent:-9.35pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Benchmarking
of compensation against our peers;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Annual
and long-term compensation based on multiple metrics tied to our short-term and
long-term goals;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Ability
of the Compensation Committee to reduce incentive compensation that otherwise
would be awarded;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Internal
controls and procedures, tied to our business ethics policy, designed to detect
improper conduct that could have a material adverse effect on Kroger;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Independent
Compensation Committee oversight of compensation policies and practices, and
determination of compensation awards to be made to senior management (except in
the case of our CEO, for whom the independent members of the board of directors
as a whole act); and</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Adoption
of a robust &#147;clawback&#148; policy, more particularly described on page&nbsp;29 of
our definitive proxy statement, under which Kroger can recover incentive
payments made to executive officers based on material errors of facts.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\105627\10-14138-1\task4187636\14138-1-bi-03.htm',USER='105627',CD='Jul 15 21:39 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the foregoing reasons, Kroger has concluded that
the risks associated with our compensation policies and practices are not
reasonably likely to have a material adverse effect on Kroger.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Performance-Based Long-Term Cash Bonus, page&nbsp;26</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We note that
under the 2008 plan participants receive a 1% payout based on improvement in
associate engagement measures.&#160; Please
describe in greater detail the &#147;associate engagement measures&#148; and what
improvement is required in order for participants to receive the 1% payout.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger Response</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger&#146;s associate engagement measures are part of a
business strategy often referred to as Associate 1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">st</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">.&#160; Kroger refers the staff to its letter dated December&nbsp;11,
2008, in response to the staff&#146;s comment letter dated October&nbsp;16, 2008,
pertaining to the same subject matter.&#160;
Kroger sought confidential treatment for that response, and received a
closure letter dated January&nbsp;8, 2009, from the staff.&#160; Continued confidential treatment of these
performance metrics and the manner in which a payout is calculated is warranted
as they constitute confidential commercial and financial information that, if
disclosed, could be used by competitors in a manner that would cause
substantial competitive harm to Kroger.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We acknowledge that:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 9.35pt;text-indent:-9.35pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">the
company is responsible for the adequacy and accuracy of the disclosure in the
filings;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">staff
comments or changes to disclosure in response to staff comments do not
foreclose the&#160;&#160; Commission from taking
any action with respect to the filings; and</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">the
company may not assert staff comments as a defense in any proceeding initiated
by the Commission or any person under the federal securities laws of the United
States.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If you have any questions or require any additional
information regarding this matter, please contact me at 513-762-1482.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
